<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Robert Louis Stevenson</h1>			<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
				<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>				<div id="contentSub"></div>
				<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>				<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
				<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p class="mw-empty-elt">

</p>
<table class="infobox vcard" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold"><span class="fn">Robert Louis Stevenson</span></th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<a href="/wiki/File:Robert_Louis_Stevenson_by_Henry_Walter_Barnett_bw.jpg" class="image" title="Robert Louis Stevenson in 1893 by Henry Walter Barnett"><img alt="Robert Louis Stevenson in 1893 by Henry Walter Barnett" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Robert_Louis_Stevenson_by_Henry_Walter_Barnett_bw.jpg/220px-Robert_Louis_Stevenson_by_Henry_Walter_Barnett_bw.jpg" width="220" height="293" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Robert_Louis_Stevenson_by_Henry_Walter_Barnett_bw.jpg/330px-Robert_Louis_Stevenson_by_Henry_Walter_Barnett_bw.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Robert_Louis_Stevenson_by_Henry_Walter_Barnett_bw.jpg/440px-Robert_Louis_Stevenson_by_Henry_Walter_Barnett_bw.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1066" data-file-height="1422" /></a><div>Robert Louis Stevenson in 1893 by <a href="/wiki/Henry_Walter_Barnett" title="Henry Walter Barnett">Henry Walter Barnett</a></div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="padding-top:0.225em;line-height:1.1em;padding-right:0.65em;">Born</th><td style="line-height:1.4em;">
Robert Lewis Balfour Stevenson<br /><span style="display:none">(<span class="bday">1850-11-13</span>)</span>13 November 1850<br /><a href="/wiki/Edinburgh" title="Edinburgh">Edinburgh</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="padding-top:0.225em;line-height:1.1em;padding-right:0.65em;">Died</th><td style="line-height:1.4em;">
3 December 1894<span style="display:none">(1894-12-03)</span> (aged&#160;44)<br /><a href="/wiki/Vailima,_Samoa" title="Vailima, Samoa">Vailima</a>, <a href="/wiki/Samoan_Islands" title="Samoan Islands">Samoan Islands</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="padding-top:0.225em;line-height:1.1em;padding-right:0.65em;">Occupation</th><td class="role" style="line-height:1.4em;">
Novelist, poet, travel writer</td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="padding-top:0.225em;line-height:1.1em;padding-right:0.65em;">Nationality</th><td class="category" style="line-height:1.4em;">
Scottish</td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="padding-top:0.225em;line-height:1.1em;padding-right:0.65em;">Citizenship</th><td style="line-height:1.4em;">
United Kingdom</td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="padding-top:0.225em;line-height:1.1em;padding-right:0.65em;">Education</th><td style="line-height:1.4em;">
1857 Mr. Henderson's School, Edinburgh<br />1857 Private tutors<br />1859 Return to Mr. Henderson's School<br />1861 <a href="/wiki/Edinburgh_Academy" title="Edinburgh Academy">Edinburgh Academy</a><br />1863 Boarding school in <a href="/wiki/Isleworth" title="Isleworth">Isleworth</a>, Middlesex<br />1864 Robert Thomson's School, Edinburgh<br />1867 <a href="/wiki/University_of_Edinburgh" title="University of Edinburgh">University of Edinburgh</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="padding-top:0.225em;line-height:1.1em;padding-right:0.65em;">Period</th><td style="line-height:1.4em;">
<a href="/wiki/Victorian_era" title="Victorian era">Victorian era</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="padding-top:0.225em;line-height:1.1em;padding-right:0.65em;">Notable works</th><td style="line-height:1.4em;">
<i><a href="/wiki/Treasure_Island" title="Treasure Island">Treasure Island</a></i><br /><i><a href="/wiki/A_Child%27s_Garden_of_Verses" title="A Child&#39;s Garden of Verses">A Child's Garden of Verses</a></i><br /><i><a href="/wiki/Kidnapped_(novel)" title="Kidnapped (novel)">Kidnapped</a></i><br /><i><a href="/wiki/Strange_Case_of_Dr_Jekyll_and_Mr_Hyde" title="Strange Case of Dr Jekyll and Mr Hyde">Strange Case of Dr Jekyll and Mr Hyde</a></i></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="padding-top:0.225em;line-height:1.1em;padding-right:0.65em;">Spouse</th><td style="line-height:1.4em;">
<a href="/wiki/Fanny_Van_de_Grift" class="mw-redirect" title="Fanny Van de Grift">Fanny Van de Grift Osbourne</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="padding-top:0.225em;line-height:1.1em;padding-right:0.65em;">Relatives</th><td style="line-height:1.4em;">
<a href="/wiki/Thomas_Stevenson" title="Thomas Stevenson">Thomas Stevenson</a> (father)<br />Margaret Isabella Balfour (mother)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Robert Louis Balfour Stevenson</b> (13 November 1850 – 3 December 1894) was a <a href="/wiki/Scottish_people" title="Scottish people">Scottish</a> novelist, poet, essayist, musician and <a href="/wiki/Travel_writing" class="mw-redirect" title="Travel writing">travel writer</a>. His most famous works are <i><a href="/wiki/Treasure_Island" title="Treasure Island">Treasure Island</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Kidnapped_(novel)" title="Kidnapped (novel)">Kidnapped</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Strange_Case_of_Dr_Jekyll_and_Mr_Hyde" title="Strange Case of Dr Jekyll and Mr Hyde">Strange Case of Dr Jekyll and Mr Hyde</a>,</i> and <i><a href="/wiki/A_Child%27s_Garden_of_Verses" title="A Child&#39;s Garden of Verses">A Child's Garden of Verses</a></i>. Stevenson was a literary celebrity during his lifetime, and now ranks as the 26th most translated author in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-indextrans_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-indextrans-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> His works have been admired by many other writers, including <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Luis_Borges" title="Jorge Luis Borges">Jorge Luis Borges</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bertolt_Brecht" title="Bertolt Brecht">Bertolt Brecht</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marcel_Proust" title="Marcel Proust">Marcel Proust</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Conan_Doyle" title="Arthur Conan Doyle">Arthur Conan Doyle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Henry_James" title="Henry James">Henry James</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cesare_Pavese" title="Cesare Pavese">Cesare Pavese</a>, <a href="/wiki/Emilio_Salgari" title="Emilio Salgari">Emilio Salgari</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Hemingway" title="Ernest Hemingway">Ernest Hemingway</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rudyard_Kipling" title="Rudyard Kipling">Rudyard Kipling</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jack_London" title="Jack London">Jack London</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Nabokov" title="Vladimir Nabokov">Vladimir Nabokov</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/J._M._Barrie" title="J. M. Barrie">J. M. Barrie</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Chaney_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chaney-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/G._K._Chesterton" title="G. K. Chesterton">G. K. Chesterton</a>, who said that Stevenson "seemed to pick the right word up on the point of his pen, like a man playing <a href="/wiki/Spillikins" class="mw-redirect" title="Spillikins">spillikins</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Childhood_and_youth">Childhood and youth</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Robert_Louis_Stevenson&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Childhood and youth">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
